........................................................................................................................MHSML  ////// MHSML: Fire incident at New Spinning warehouse  ////// (Continuation news of MHSML): After recognizer the fire safety team of the Company started their fire fighter as well fire service reached at the affected area immediately. With the help of 04 unit fire service defense authority, the fire got under control after 6/7 hours. The approximate loss estimated BDT 15.00 crore. The Company also informed that all the Row Cotton, Finished Yarn and warehouse Shed are under insurance coverage and appointed surveyor of the insurance company doing the survey. (end)  /////// 2021-02-28
........................................................................................................................MHSML  ////// MHSML: Fire incident at New Spinning warehouse  ////// The Company has informed that an accidental fire hazard happened at New Spinning warehouse (Ring unit) of the Company.
